 Labor Day 2019 is celebrated with great enthusiasm every year

 Labor Day is also called Labor Day, May Day 2019, Labor Day

 This day is a holiday in almost all companies of the country
 sirf bharat hi nahin duniya ke kareeb 80 deshon main is din rashtriya avkaash rahata he
 Labor Day in India is celebrated in honor of working people
 bharat main majdoordivas manaaneki shuruyatsbase pehle chennai main 1 may 1923 ko hui thi
 At that time it was authenticated as Madras Day
 is kii shuruyaat bhartiya majdoor kisaan party ke netaa kamred singravelu chetyar ne shuru kii thi

 The Sunrisers Hyderabad team defeated Delhi Daredevils by three wickets in the 14th match of the sixth edition of the Indian Premier League (IPL) released on Friday at the Ferozeshah Kotla ground
 mejabaan team kii yah lagaataar chauthi haar he jabaki sunrisers ne teesri jeet darj kii he
 This low-scoring match was made difficult by the Sunrisers batsmen due to their poor batting
 yahi kaaran he ki unhen tamaam prayaason ke baad 20wein over main saat wicket ganvaakar jeet mili
 Dale Steyn, returning David Warner to the pavilion on the fourth ball of the innings, hit the winning four
 sten nau ranon par naabad rahe jabaki amit mishra ek ahm pari khelte hue 16 ranon par naabad laute
 Mishra hit two fours off 14 balls
 dairedevills kii tarah sunrisers kii shuruyaat bhi acchhee nahin rahi thi
 Shahbaz Nadeem gave the Daredevils a comfortable start by running out Akshat Reddy (1) on a two-run total but Parthiv Patel (19) and captain Kumar Sangakkara (28) added 44 runs for the second wicket to reduce the grief
 did
 parthiv 46 ranon ke kul yoga par nadeem kii gend par unheen ke haathon lapke gaye
 Parthiv hit four boundaries off 19 balls
 iske baad sangakaara ne hanuma vihari (17) ke saath score ko 54 tak pahunchaaya lekin is yoga par johaan botha ne sangakaara ko out karke apni team kii phir se match main vaapasi karai
 Now the Daredevils had a chance to hold on to the match
 is maukey ko bhunaate hue nadeem ne 69 ranon ke kul yoga par camran white (4) ko kedaar jadhav ke haathon stump karaayaa
 White's wicket fell on the last ball of the 14th over
 morne morkal ne 15wein over kii duusari gend par vihari ko botha ke haathon kaich karakar apni team ko paanchavin safalataa dilaai
 Ashish Reddy (16) then brought his team back into the match again with two fours in Umesh Yadav's over but he was bowled in the first ball of the 17th over bowled by Morkel in an attempt to play a wrong shot
 mishra ne morkal ke us over main ek no ball sahit aath ran lekar isaki samaapti tak aankade ko 18 gendon par 18 ranon tak pahunchaa diya
 At the other end, Thisira Perera was waiting for his turn after playing just two balls
 bade shots khilne ke liye mashhoor perera ne ab tak sirf do gendon kaa saamana kiya tha
 On the first ball of the 18th over bowled by Irfan Pathan, the Daredevils team accused Mishra of deliberately getting in the way of the ball thrown towards the wicket but the umpire Aleem Dar denied it
 duusari gend khaali jane ke baad teesri gend par mishra ne ek ran liya or is tarah perera strike par laute
 Perera attempted to fly a Pathan ball over long on but was caught by Botha at the boundary line
 vah do ran hi bana sake
 His wicket fell at a total of 100 runs
 antim 12 gendon par sunrisers ko 12 ran banane the

 is tarah sunrisers ko antim over main jeet ke liye chah ranon kii darkaar thi

 pehali gend par sten ne do ran liye or duusari gend par chaukaa lagaakar apni team kii jeet pakki kii

 botha or pathan ko ek-ek wicket mila
 Earlier, the Daredevils team, who came out to bat first after winning the toss, could only manage 114 for eight in the allotted 20 overs due to the failure of their three veterans - David Warner, Virender Sehwag and captain Mahela Jayawardene
 kedaar jadhav ne sabase adhik naabad 30 ran banaae jabaki irfan pathan ne 23 ranon kaa yogadan diya

 Sehwag hit two fours off 10 balls while the captain was dismissed with a four and a six off 14 balls
 iske baad johaan botha (9) or manpreet juneja (15) ne score ko 44 ranon tak pahunchaaya lekin isi yoga par anand rajan ne ko out kar dilli ko chauthaa jhatka diya

 botha or pathan ko ek-ek wicket mila
 Earlier, the Daredevils team, who came out to bat first after winning the toss, could only manage 114 for eight in the allotted 20 overs due to the failure of their three veterans - David Warner, Virender Sehwag and captain Mahela Jayawardene
 kedaar jadhav ne sabase adhik naabad 30 ran banaae jabaki irfan pathan ne 23 ranon kaa yogadan diya
 Warner could not even open the account while Sehwag and Jayawardene could only score 12-12 runs
 mejabaan team kii shuruyaat behad kharaab rahi
 First Warner (0) departed
 sunrisers ke dakshin africa express del sten ne pari kii chauthi gend par hi warner ko pavilion kii raah dikhaa di
 After this it seemed that Sehwag and Jayawardene would make up for this loss
 donon ne duusare wicket ke liye 26 ran jode lekin ishanth sharma ne paanchaven over kii teesri gend par jayavardhane or chauthi gend par sahvaag ko chalata kar yah sabit kiya ki dilli ke dabang ab sahvaag nahin balki vah hai
 Sehwag hit two fours off 10 balls while the captain was dismissed with a four and a six off 14 balls
 iske baad johaan botha (9) or manpreet juneja (15) ne score ko 44 ranon tak pahunchaaya lekin isi yoga par anand rajan ne ko out kar dilli ko chauthaa jhatka diya
 Juneja and Irfan tried to maintain the situation by sharing 21 runs for the fifth wicket but on the total of 65 runs, Amit Mishra caught Juneja by Cameron White
 juneja ne 22 gendon kaa saamana kiya
 Pathan and Jadhav now had the responsibility of bringing the team total to over 100
 donon ne iske liye bharpoor prayaas kiya lekin 95 ke kul yoga par pathan out ho gaye
 There was a 30-run partnership between the two
 pathan ne 30 gendon par ek chaukaa lagaaya

 iske baad perera ne 96 ke kul yoga par morne morkal (0) ko out kar diya
 The comments rahi-sahi kasar sten ne pari ke 19wein over kii duusari gend par shahzad nadeem (0) ko bold karke puri kar di
 This wicket fell at a total of 98
 sten ne ipel-6 kaa ab tak kii sabase kifayati gendbaaji karte hue chaar over main ek madan sahit 11 ran dekar do wicket liye
 After this however, Jadhav and Yadav did not allow any more damage and added 16 runs for the final wicket
 jadhav ne 20 gendon par ek chaukaa or do chakke lagaae
 Ishant, Perera and Stan took two wickets each for Sunrisers while Rajan and Mishra got one each
 mishra ne morkal ke us over main ek no ball sahit aath ran lekar isaki samaapti tak aankade ko 18 gendon par 18 ranon tak pahunchaa diya
 At the other end, Thisira Perera was waiting for his turn after playing just two balls
 bade shots khilne ke liye mashhoor perera ne ab tak sirf do gendon kaa saamana kiya tha

 duusari gend khaali jane ke baad teesri gend par mishra ne ek ran liya or is tarah perera strike par laute

 Spain's leading female tennis player Conchita Martinez managed to win just one Grand Slam title while active in tennis, but as a Davis Cup captain she now wants to fill that gap by winning Spain the Davis Cup title
 konchita 1994 main wimbledon main mahila ekal varg kii champion rah chuki hai, jahaan unhone america diggaj martina navaratilova ko final main maat di thi
 In addition, she was runner-up at the Australian Open in 1998 and the French Open in 2000
 bharat ke khilaaf davis cap world group plaof muqabla khilne ai spanish team kii gaiyr-pratispardhi captain evam purv duusari vishwa variyata praapt konchita ab bataur coach safalataa arjeet karnaa chaahati hai
 "I would have been better if i could have won more titles while i was active in tennis," Conchita said in an interview to IANS on Wednesday during the Spanish team's practice session in preparation for the Davis Cup
 maine khelte hue wimbledon jeeta, haalanki main or grand slam khitaab jeetna chaahati thi
 " konchita ne kaha, "lekin ab main coach ban chuki hum
 i want to earn more success as a coach than as successful as a player

 ) Conchita has been a women's singles champion at Wimbledon in 1994, where she defeated American stalwart Martina Navratilova in the final
 iske alaava vah 1998 main australian open or 2000 main french open main up-vijeta raheen
 The Spanish team's non-competitive captain and former second-world seeded Conchita, who came to play Davis Cup World Group playoff against India, now wants to succeed as a coach
 konchita ne davis cap kii taiyaariyon main juty spanish team ke abhyaas satr ke dauraan buudhvaar ko ieenes ko die saakshaatkaar main kaha, "main tennis main sakriy rahane ke dauraan yadi or khitaab jeet paati to acha rahata
 i won Wimbledon while playing, though i wanted to win more Grand Slam titles
 " Konchita said, "but now i have become a coach
 main ek khilaadi ke taur par jitani safal rahi usase kahin adhik safalataa bataur coach arjeet karnaa chaahati hum
 Our main goal is to return to the Davis Cup World Group and hope to win the Davis Cup title as well
 " The 44-year-old Conchita has also been appointed as the non-competitive captain of Spain's Fed Cup and she is enjoying her career as a coach these days
 konchita ne kaha, "yah bilkul juda ahsaas he
 Now i know that my return as a player is not possible, so i am enjoying my responsibilities as a coach
 hamaare paas rafel nadal or david pherar jaise dhurandhar khilaadiyon se las behtareen team he, jisase meraa kaam kaaphi aasaan ho jaataa he
 " haalanki konchita ne yah bhi sweekaar kiya ki bharat ke khilaaf davis cap main khelte hue spanish khilaadiyon ko dilli kii garmi pareshaan karegi

 unhone kaha, "yahaan kaa vaataavaran kaaphi kathin he

 ) Apart from the Shivalayas of Patna, Bihar's capital, the hill temple of Ranchi, the capital of Jharkhand, has also been attracting devotees since morning and people are praying to Lord Shiva and wishing for their happy future

 Here, devotees have also gathered in all the Shivalayas, including Baba Garibarnath Temple of Muzaffarpur, Bihar, Someshwar Temple in Motihari, Guptadham Temple of Rohtas, Hariharanath Temple of Sonepur, Ajgabinath Temple, Vasukinath Temple in Jharkhand
 vam morcha tripura vidhansabha main shandaar jeet hasil karte hue rajya main paanchavin baar sattashin hone ja rahaa he
 The election results on Thursday have shocked everyone
 vam morche ne vidhansabha kii 60 main se 50 par kabja jamaa liya he jabaki pratipakshi congress ko mahaj 10 siton se santosh karnaa padaa
 Workers of leftist parties, especially the Communist Party of india-marxist (CPI-M), have been celebrating across the state after the election results came out, while the Congress camp was silent
 makapa ne 49 siton par jeet darj kii, jabaki uski sahyogi bhartiya communist party (bhakpa) ne ek seat par jeet hasil kii he
 This result has proved to be better for the Left Front after 1978
 1978 main morcha ne 56 siton par jeet hasil kii thi
 The Morcha has won one seat more this time than in the 2008 assembly elections
 jeet se prasann mukhyamantri maanik sarkaar ne kaha, "logon ne vikaas, shanti or sthayitv ke alaava sushasan ke paksh main matdaan kiya
 " varsh 1998 se hi rajya main shashan chalaa rahe 64 varshiya maanik sarkaar dhanpur seat se chhathi baar jite hai
 He is the only leader who will hold the post of Chief Minister of Tripura for the fourth time
 congress jahaan maatr 10 siten barkaraar rakhane main kaamyaab rahi, vahiin uski sahyogi indiinas nesanalist party of tripura (aienpiti) ko niraashaa haath lagi he
 It won one seat five years ago
 trinmul congress ne 2008 main 22 pratyaashee maidan main utaare the, lekin gaiyr vaamo maton ke vibhaajan ko rokane ke liye is baar ke chunaav main usne ek bhi pratyaashee khadaa nahin kiya
 However, the Congress did not get the benefit of going to its 'backfoot'
 tippaniyan 75-year-old teacher-turned-politician Anil Sarkar is also a poet and writer
 unhone nauveen baar chunaav jitkar record kaayam kiya
 He has been re-elected from Pratapgarh in western Tripura on a CPI-M ticket
 ullekhneey he ki tripura main vam morcha 1978 se hi satta par kabiz he
 This front had been away from power only once (during 1988–93)
 chunaav parinaam saamne aane ke baad vampanthi partiyon, khaskar marxvaadi communist party (makapa) ke kaaryakarta puure rajya main utsav manaa rahe hai, jabaki congress ke kheme main sannata pasra hua he
 The CPI (M) won 49 seats, while its ally Communist Party of India (CPI) won one seat
 1978 ke baad vam morcha ke liye is baar kaa parinaam behatar sabit hua he
 In 1978, the Morcha won 56 seats
 2008 ke vidhansabh chunaav ke mukaable morcha ne is baar ek seat zyada jiti he
 Pleased with the victory, Chief Minister Manik Sarkar said, “people voted in favor of good governance apart from development, peace and stability
 " Manik Sarkar, 64, who has been ruling the state since 1998, has won the Dhanpur seat for the sixth time
 ve akele aise netaa hai jo chauthi baar tripura ke mukhyamantri pad par kabiz honge
 While the Congress managed to retain only 10 seats, its ally Indigenous Nationalist Party of Tripura (INPT) has been disappointed
 paanch saal pehle isane ek seat par jeet hasil kii thi
 The Trinamool Congress fielded 22 candidates in 2008, but it did not field a single candidate in this election to prevent the division of non-lf votes
 uske 'baikfoot' par jane kaa bhi haalanki congress ko phayda nahin mil paaya
 The comments shikshak se rajaneta bane 75 varshiya anil sarkaar kavi or lekhak bhi hai
 He set the record by winning the election for the ninth time
 vah makapa ke tikat par pashchimi tripura ke pratapgarh se phir nirvaachit hue hai
 It is noteworthy that the Left Front has been in power in Tripura since 1978
 yah morcha sirf ek baar (1988-93 ke dauraan) satta se dur rahaa tha

 Traveling to Indori Pohe Poha is more commonly eaten in Maharashtra and Madhya Pradesh
 madhya pradesh main bhi khaskar malwa ilaake main
 There are many stories about its history
 lekin indore main poha desh kii aazaadee ke kareeb do saal baad dastak de chukaa tha
 Purushottam Joshi, who lives in Raigad, Maharashtra, came to Indore with his aunt
 is dauraan vah ek company main slesman kii job bhi karte the
 During that time Joshi came to mind that the idea of opening a Pohe shop
 phir kya tha, purushottam ne indore main apni pohe kii dukaan khol di
 After which Pohe trend in Indore continued to grow
 chuki poha dhan se banataa he or ek samay main chhattisgarh madhya pradesh kaa hissaa hua karata tha
 Due to the high crop of paddy, it started to be used in many ways
 jisamen se ek poha tha
 Poha in Indore is different from other places? Poha is spicy and has a healthy breakfast
 aamator par log ise normal sabji kii tarah baghaar kar banaate hai
 But in Indore it is made in a different way
 pohe ko do-teen baar pani se dhokar isamen haldi daalkar kuch der ke liye chhod diya jaataa he (pani main bhingo diya jaataa he)
 Then a pot of rye, curry leaves, peanut and light chilli is prepared, then it is cooked by mixing it in a kneaded poha and keeping it on top of a pan filled with water
 poha pani kii bhaap main garm hone ke saath-saath pakataa bhi he
 Then two types of sev are put in it
 ek to moti jo ki tikhi seve hoti he, moti seve ke saath isamen tikhi bundi bhi daali jaati he
 The second serving is fine and does not contain chilli
 saath hi isamen baarik kataa hua pyaaj, haraa dhaniya, neembu kaa ras, anaar ke dane or upar se jiravan chhidakar saath main garma-garam jalebi ke saath khaaya jaataa he
 Seeing, reading and writing all these things is bound to come in everyone's mouth
 to ye he naa baaki jagahon se alag
 This is what makes it different, and then every city has its own taste
 ek report ke mutabik, indore ke thok bazaar se rojaanaa kareeb-kareeb 65 ton pohe kii bikri hoti he
 Pohe is mostly produced in Ujjain and Chhattisgarh
 lekin isaki sabase zyada khapat indore or phir sampurna malwa ilaake main hoti he
 It is preferred in many states along with Madhya Pradesh and Maharashtra
 upi, rajasthan, chhattisgarh, dilli-ensiaar main bhi khaaya jaataa he
 But it is different that they are not fun in taste which are in Pohe of Indore
 pohe tere kitne nampohe ko alag-alag pradeshon yaa jagahon par anek naamon se janaa jaataa he
 In Maharashtra and MP it is known as Pohe
 pohe ko peeta chaaval or chapata chaaval ke naam se bhi janaa jaataa he
 It is known as Attu in Telugu, Chida in Bengal and Assam, Chiura or Chuda in areas of Bihar- Jharkhand and in Gujarati it is known as Paua
 saath hi ise har jagah alag-alag tareeke se banaaya jaataa he
 In many places it is eaten by mixing sugar with milk which is called milk-poha
 to vahiin kerala ke said ise nariyal or kele ke saath banaaya jaataa he
 Also, it is fried and eaten as a chivda in many places
 bihar main, khaskar mithila ilaake main dahi ke saath chuda khaanaa bahut pasand kiya jaataa he
 Chuda is also eaten with sattu in areas of Magadha
 indore main poha diwas7 june ko indore main vishwa poha diwas banaaya jaataa he
 It was initiated by the artist Rajiv Nema of Indore, who is living abroad nowadays
 is din indore main jagah-jagah poha or jalebi kaa vitaran hota he or soshal media ke jariye deshbhar main iske bare main bataaya jaataa he
 In the GI tag race, Pohe's name recommends the name of GI Tag (geographical Index Tag) for four more things, including Indo Ka Poha
 jinamein poha, laung senv, khatta-meetha namakeen or doodh se banaai jane vaali shikanji he
 The state government also announced the branding of poha-jalebi and namkeen in the budget
 haalanki kareeb chah maheene pehle jiaai tag kii prakriya shuru ho chuki he
 What is a GI tag? Geographical index tag is one of the products to which a place's identity is attached
 ise milane ke baad koi vyakti yaa phir sanstha use apana nahin bataa sakati hai
 So in total, came to Indore and did not eat poha, then what did you eat
 khaane main lavaabadar to he hi saath-saath yah healdi bhi he
 It is also digested quickly
 to chalate-chalate ham aapako bataa dente hai ki agar aap bhi indore jaaen to in dukaanon main pohe kaa swaad jarur chakhen
